<user_name>Justajoe4u</user_name><Date>1577229657396<//Date><Rate>3<//Rate><Review>Been here about 20 times and so figured it was time for a review. They can have you out in 45 minutes or they can take as long as 6 hours that‚Äôs been my experience for the most part they‚Äôll get you out within two hours but if you see a lot of trucks on the docks be prepared to wait. They have about 30 docks they use to live unload and if you about 20-25 trucks already docked just expect to wait quite a while. The process is fairly simple, it‚Äôs one truck at a time, make sure you have your reflective vest on at all times, guard will assign a door you park the truck at said door and then turn in your paper work at the office. Go back to your truck and once the light is green you are good to go. If your freight is not pre paid you will have to wait for lumper to call you and give you a total for unloading freight. So very simple process and easy in and out it‚Äôs just the unloading process that can sometimes take forever, so hopefully you have better luck than not.< /Review><Pics>None<//Pics>< response>

< text>
So first all I would like to give a huge thank you to platinum banquet and their team. I am very happy how everything turned out.
So my sister's quinceanera was this last Saturday. They let us enter the hall at 10 am to prep everything that we needed to do. Like the candy bar the decorations and also the photographer was able to check the dvd player and we had no problems at all. My sister was also able to practice before the actuall dance so that was great.
I met the manger who in charge and he explained everything. Mind you my parents don't speak Spanish so I had to translate. But he explained that 10 mins before they open the buffet they would feed the quinceanera and the crew. Which was so fancy i actually loved it. And we talked about the timing of cutting the cake and the passing for the toast and ECT. He was so helpful. We didn't have plates for the candy bar and he was so nice to give us some. And when I had questions he was always nice about anwsering even if I asked twice. Also the security guard introduce himself and basically explained what his job indicated like the list and If there were to be a problem he would first come to me then if the problem wasn't resolved then he would take furher action. But there was no problems at all. So they were both very helpful and both very nice people. Also the servers were great. Every time I asked for something they would answer and just do what I would ask. Very nice people too. Very please with the management and their team all so helpful with great attitudes.
Now the food was okay. I personally liked it some dishes were good others were not. My family was not a fan. But I think as Latinos were not used to the type of food they provide But like I said they had many options some dishes were great others were not but the food was worth paying for less stress to worry about. Also what banquet halls provide great food. Lmk because I been to many and they all seem the same.  Also they provide chips with salsa, fruits as well. And now for the beer. I was so happy knowing we were able to bring as much as we wanted. And we were not charge for extra. We had the option of a open bar but we kept it simple so I am very please with that as well. Overall i was very happy with everything I would definitely recommend this hall to you and my friends to my family.  If you decided to book this hall please book in advance even a year in advance. We were planning for the summer but there were no more openings. We also thought no one would show up because of the timing but everyone showed up.
Also so y'all know the cost of the party. We had 300 guest. It included food, drinks, cake, fruit and the photographer which you had to pay for the pictures. But many people bought which was nice because they had a memory to take home. It didn't bother me at all. It was their hustle you have to respect that. But overall it was about 10 grand. But it is all different depending on the timing also how many guesy so just call and ask for an estimate. I also loved the fact that the owner was chill about the payments he allowed us to pay the the last payment a day before the party and he wasn't rude about it. And he was also very helpful and nice about everything. We will be booking the place in the future. And So once again thank you for everything. Less stress. Once it hits 12 am we picked up our last belongings. The banda was also picking up there things. No one rushed us.
I am so happy with everything!!!! Thank you again<//text>

< Text>
Out of an hour long class they frequently spend 40 minutes on solo work. During this time the only instruction is watching the instructor dance in the front of the room. If you do not get what the instructor is doing you will not be corrected or have an opportunity to ask a question. The music just keeps going and you just have to try again when the instructor repeats the movement.

Then they switch to partner work. The partner work instruction is adequate in quality, but the remaining 20 minutes is insufficient to fully grasp the partner sequence.

Ultimately there is very little correction if you are doing something wrong.

This is better than some studios, but no where near as good as a studio can be. They do not deserve the 1 star rating I‚Äôm giving them, but they also do not deserve the 5 star rating they have maintained. If their overall rating was 4 stars I think that would more accurately reflect the studio.

My suggestion for improvement would be to either place the solo work in a separate class or to reduce the amount of curriculum covered in a class so that it can be done properly.< /Text>

David and his crew at Majesty in Motion are absolutely phenomenal!
My fianc√© and I decided to try out salsa dancing on a whim last January and ended up at Tango Del Rey on a Friday evening. The first hour of the night was a class hosted by David and that was our first exposure to salsa. Needless to say, we had a great time and began taking classes at the studio soon after.

Since then, I have danced in Mexico, Peru, Boston, and NY and NONE of the classes I have taken can compare to our experience at Majesty in Motion. David and his instructors are not only great dancers themselves, but they are one with the dance. As instructors, they understand the physical and mental blocks of their students better than the students themselves and this is the defining characteristic of great teachers and the single most important quality that has allowed us to progress as well as we have with this dance company.

Joining the salsa team has positively impacted my life in ways I could have never imagined. Never having danced before in my entire life, it's an honor to be a part of a team comprised of such motivating, talented, and charismatic individuals.

To be honest, the thought of learning how to dance first terrified me. Letting the music move you is easier said than done.I was terrified that I would never be good enough. I didn‚Äôt know how to dance. I thought I would "fail". So I held on tighter, tensed up, got stiff.

David and Jennifer have taught me that the music‚Äôs always playing. We just have to decide if we‚Äôre still going to hold ourselves back, or if we‚Äôre going to dance. Try it yourself. Let go of those reigns. Give in. Surrender. Feel the music. Feel the rhythm. And then, when you‚Äôre ready, let it carry you. Let it move you.

We look forward to dancing around the world, but we'll always find ourselves back at Majesty!< /review>

The best place to learn Salsa and Bachata!!!

I have danced for Majesty in Motion for the past two years and I have got to say, it has changed my life. I learned everything I know about Salsa and Bachata from David, Jennifer, Patrick, Robbie, Eva and Gonzalo. All the instructors I have encountered at Majesty have been so helpful and are wonderful human beings.

What I like about Majesty is that they focus a lot on technique, timing and body movement which are the keys to social dancing. I have looked into other dance studios in San Diego and this is hands down the best place to learn.

Majesty has become my family and they have made me feel so welcomed in the Salsa dancing community.</review>

< review>
Lived there for ~9 months, early terminated to move back to south bay.

Good:
- Good price in this area
- 90% Quiet & good structure to block outside noise
- Staff is good.
- Good gym with squat machine - better than south bay ones.

Bad:
-2 inner-noise. The exhausting pipe is connected to neighbor's living room. They had a crying baby at 6am. And suddenly it became my problem and disrupted my sleep. They should either offer discount or allow people to know what family composition is in their neighbor. Imaging flying a overnight plane every night with a crying baby onboard.
- $300 parking fee - well, it is SF. can't blame anyone
- Still pricy, but it is SF</review>

A Lovely Place to Live, With Super Service and Personnel

Rincon Green Apartments is a great place to call home. The community is extremely beautiful, well-kept and peaceful. In fact, everything is so beautiful that I felt like I lived at a resort. The staff always greet residents with a smile, are very attentive to their needs and are quick to attend to any problems that arise. I would like to give special kudos to maintenance worker Andrew and property managers Laila and Janae. Once, I spilled laundry detergent on my apartment's carpet, and I was in a panic because I really don't like the sticky, messy feeling of the laundry detergent residue. I submitted the service request in the morning and Andrew helped me do a deep cleaning of the entire apartment's carpet the same day! What an awesome service! Laila and Janae from the leasing office are super helpful and accommodating. They always try their best to make residents' stay in the community as comfortable as possible. My initial apartment was faced the street, and I couldn't get used to the noise. After learning about the issue, Laila and Janae immediately transferred me to a quiet courtyard apartment at a discounted price. My sleeping quality has since improved significantly!

The apartment could not be in a better location and is close to many shops, grocery stores, restaurants, cafes, bars and transportation options. It offers some of the most cutting-edge designs and boutique amenities in the area. Amenities include a community park, rooftop lounge with a hot tub and grill (I have thrown two BBQ parties here, and my guests had a great time and were extremely satisfied), a 24-hour fitness center, concierge and cyber caf√©, on-site Zipcar and panoramic city views. The apartment is within walking distance of the downtown financial district, SOMA, Google, Facebook, Salesforce, Visa, MasterCard, and all the major tech companies. It is also just a10-minute walk to Embarcadero Boulevard, where you can enjoy breathtaking views of the bay and the Bay Bridge!

In summary, I really enjoyed my time here, as the apartment was very clean, comfortable and had everything I could need! In addition, the maintenance worker is super-efficient, and the office staff are friendly. I will always recommend this fabulous apartment to others!<//Review>

<text>We love living here so much that we have recently renewed our lease. Although it is not cheap to live here, we appreciate all the valuable services that this building provides, at a very reasonable rate. You could surely get cheaper, but you will have to deal with shady landlords.

Rincon Green is run by Emerald Fund, who have the most fantastic staff: Laila and Vanessa manage the building, while Sarah and Emyli are the friendliest leasing agents around. Make sure you tell them about my review. They organize monthly get-togethers to introduce you to your neighbours. Joey and Cameron watch over the concierge desk during the day, making sure to sign for our deliveries and greeting guests. At nights, there is very friendly security and the park gates are locked. Jerry and Jairell are maintenance and they make sure everything is in tip-top shape. It's a new building, built in 2012, but when we had trouble with the heat and plumbing, they showed up right away!

The building is really lovely, there's Emerald Park as our front yard, with a playground for the little ones to climb on. Inside the building, there's a courtyard with a rock garden and water fountain. If you get a unit with a balcony, it's easy to forget you are actually living in a big city. There is free Philz coffee in the morning, with complimentary tea throughout the day. We really enjoy using the rooftop hot tub after working out in the nice gym on the first floor. And there's also a couple of communal gas grills for quick no-mess dinners.

As for the units, they are a little small, but with good furniture a couple can live comfortably in a 1-bedroom apartment. You can find the floor plans on their website. Each unit comes with apartment-sized appliances: washer, dryer, stove and oven, microwave, and fridge. Since this is an eco-friendly building, there solar-powered heat but no air-conditioning. Since SF doesn't get that hot or cold, we keep the windows open most of the time. If you need a parking space, that's extra, but they do have ports for cars to charge.

We don't really need one, because there are three Zipcars available in the parking garage. And we ride our bikes, which are safely locked up in the storage rooms. You also get Webpass for Internet, which is speedy and reliable. They have Laundry Lockers downstairs if you want someone else to handle your clothes. You can also rent a storage locker, but I think they have a deal with Omni for on-demand storage. And they have a deal with Zeel for discounted massages.

There are a couple of disadvantages though: the sidewalks in the area are often unusable due to the condos popping up all over Rincon Hill. There is also the new Transbay Terminal that is being built, so it does get noisy on the weekends. And since it's close to the Bay Bridge, with its on- and off-ramps, traffic does back up on Harrison St.<//text>< user>

< Text>
I've been coming here nearly every workday for the last few weeks. The staff are all very friendly and inviting. I usually get tea, as opposed to coffee, but their tea is really favorful - something that always gets me going in the morning. The space is very open, with plenty of seating for the volume of customers they routinely have, most of which buy to go. I've only used their bathrooms twice, but each time the space was surprisingly clean, considering there are no locks on the doors (big difference compared to places like Starbucks which require keys or combinations to access their bathrooms).

Overall, if you are one for picking up a cup of Joe in the morning - or if you're a tea drinker like me - I definitely recommend this spot!< /Text>

< Name>
Wei Chi Kao</Name>
<time>1623217991610</time><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
Get the Quattro Salumi pizza.

This place is literally built on it: Italian pizza oven, imported Italian ingredients, and numerous awards won because of it.

Sure, the pear salad was really refreshing and balanced-and could've gotten a good review by itself-but the star is the meat lover pizza.

The neopolitan-style pizza has the satisfying  indulgence that fulfills any pizza craving. The rich cured meats is complimented by the robust and tangy tomato sauce. The airy soft crispy crust turns into nice breadsticks to scoop back every bite of umami goodness dropped.

They can also make anything gluten-free and have a wide variety of pizzas. They are all good, but the Quattro Salumi is in a league of its own.

I have been here multiple times and have never left hungry or disappointed.

5 stars for sure.<//Review>

The dough is unique and chewy. They typically don't cut the pizza either like an OG. Their pizzas are on the smaller size so order lots! < text>
This is a great place for pizza! Not your typical run-of-the-mill pizza. No. This is an artisanal type of pizza, as it is made in Naples, Italy. A thin hand-tossed, wood oven-baked pizza that is out of this world. It is meant to be eaten quickly. Why? Because the moisture of the sauce, cheese and toppings make the thin-crusted pie soggy after a while. Don't take long to eat it. Another thing I can recommend is the panini--excellent choice--served with a generous green salad. I have only been there for lunch, at which time there is no waiting. In the evening, I do not know nor can I guarantee that you won't be waiting.<//text>

I would recommend going for this menu for sure.<//Text>

<Text>Had a clement family lunch here Fuoco pizza is made at the time of your order and fired in a 1000 degrees oven---it's classic Neapolitan style cuisine from the Naples region.

Burrata is fresh creamy mozzarella from Italy and Caprese is served with sliced tomato, leafy green basil, drizzled with imported extra virgin olive oil and presented like art on white dinnerware.

12 inches are the individual size for pizza (called Pizze on menu).  Neapolitan pizza is served unsliced and may be devoured with a fork and knife. This Pizze/ Pizza is tasty and served in a warm atmosphere.</Text>< pics>

< Review>
I would like to first start by saying the food is as delicious as it is beautiful.¬† The pizza is baked to perfection; the crust is crunchy and light. The proportion of cheese and sauce are perfectly distributed with a touch of basil. I am currently enjoying the Diavola pizza (spicy salami ). By far my favorite pizza fuocos offers. Of course that varies by preference. I love spicy foods and can be plain at times. I personally think that the pizzas are best when paired with the Peach Iced tea. The sweetness of the tea balances the spice in the pizza, the tea isn't too sweet and is bottled. However, you are given a cold glass for your tea. The owner is an amazing cook and sweetheart. He comes across very serious,¬† but has given me the best service in the house, with the exception of Rosa. Rosa served me before and delivered with excellence. I am only giving a 4 star today because I felt that the waitress today was very short with me. I came for happy hour and it was 2:20, she said it wasn't 2:30pm yet and walked away. I just stood at the bar waiting with no clue if I could still order food. I am on my lunch break and don't mind paying full price. The owner however came over to ask if I had been helped and I answered "yes, i am waiting to order at 2:30 I think". By the time he asked it was 2:25pm. He went ahead and took my order and i stayed at the bar. The waitress did explain why she didn't take my order. I understood that, I just didn't appreciate the way she went about it. But maybe she was having an off day. My food was ready within 3 minutes and she brought it over. I waited about a minute for my utensils, but she didn't come back. I reached over and grabbed a pair since the were directly to my right and at reach. I will definitely come back and reccoment this place. Today was just odd, hence my four stars.</Review>

< Text>
Wow. This pizza restaurant is so much more with its family owned status and dedication to sourcing its ingredients (And pizza oven) straight from Napoli. If you are anywhere near Fullerton this is definitely the place you should be if you want to have a great meal from a great family/restaurant.
I found nothing wrong with my meal besides leaving very full, but that is definitely a good thing!

My suggestion is to get the Involtini Ai Sapori. It is prosciutto wrapped around mozzarella and arugula with pesto on the side... Amazing.</Text>

<name>MrMoruss78 Mo</name><Time>1485359643685< /Time>< rate>
4< /rate>
< Review>
Came here on a Friday night for a friends bday gathering about 8pm.  Just the tip.  This place is bussssy at this time, but the staff was so accommodating to our ever growing party of 8-12 people.  The waiter was extremely patient with us and served us always with a smile.

At dinner my friend ordered the Mozzarella bar which consists for 4 types of cheeses to choose from.  In this particular case we ordered a creamy slightly salty Burrata; reminiscent of French Brie and freshly made smoked Bufala on a bed of spicy arugula.  Not only did this plate come with these tasty cheeses, surprisingly it also came pizza size foccacia bread.

This plate was big enough to share with the table, so we decided to get our own 12 inch Affumicata thin crust Napolitean topped with smoked mozzarella, earthy roasted mushrooms, sweet tomato sauce, fresh basil and an extra drizzle of extra virgin olive oil pizza.  Our friend got a beautiful Diavola pizza with long thin strips of spicy salami, specks of crushed red pepper, mozzarella, tomato sauce and freshly picked basil. That thing looked like a piece of art!  Add a bottle of Cab, let the wine flow and we were ready to party hearty!< /Review>
